# DO NOT CHANGE THE POSITIONS OF cut_down_to_size_no_infamy, cut_down_to_size_no_add_wargoal, or status_quo - IT BREAKS WAR INTERVENTION
#
# INSTRUCTIONS:
# -------------
# constructing_cb - default to yes. if "no", cant be picked for generation or as add_wargoal if no CB already
# is_triggered_only - Triggered from within the code or by event effects. DO NOT REMOVE THE STOCK ONES.
# mutual - The CB effects will also be used by the defender in peace treaties
# months - The number of months this CB will be valid. Only works for triggered CBs.
# prerequisites - A condition that automatically activates a CB. Does not work for triggered CBs. 'THIS' scope is the target country.
# badboy_factor - Multiplied with any badboy increase normally associated with a peace option.
# prestige_factor - Multiplied with any prestige increase normally associated with a peace option.
# peace_cost_factor - Multiplied with the cost of the peace options in the peace treaty
# po_xxx - Peace options. If toggled on, badboy_factor and prestige_factor are multiplied with any associated base changes to these (see defines.txt.)
# allowed_states - If 'po_demand_states' is on, badboy_factor applies to these provinces. 'THIS' scope is us.
# on_add - effect triggered when war goal added (triggering country's scope)
# construction_speed - base modifier for how long creating this CB will take. default is 1. 1.2 means 20% faster
# great_war_obligatory - cb is always added to the peace offer/demand in great wars.
# po_remove_cores - may be used only with: po_transfer_provinces, po_demand_state, po_annex
# crisis - can be offered as a wargoal in a crisis
#
# The peace options are:
#po_annex
#po_demand_state
#po_add_to_sphere
#po_disarmament
#po_reparations
#po_transfer_provinces
#po_remove_prestige
#po_make_puppet
#po_release_puppet
#po_status_quo
#po_install_communist_gov_type
#po_uninstall_communist_gov_type
#po_remove_cores
#po_colony

# NOTE: The order in which the peace options are listed is the order in which the AI will normally prioritize them in peace treaties

# TRIGGERED - Triggered from within the code or by event effects
# --------------------------------------------------------------

# A note on naval requirements for overseas targets: `num_of_ports` has a curious behavior where
# paths from the capital to coastal provinces are computed and the final result only accounts for
# those that are reachable. (This may only apply for inland capitals.)
#
# In particular hostile sieges (including those from rebels) block those computed paths, but not
# much else does. This bears repeating: a country may be fully occupied and/or covered in *roaming*
# armies, and this won't affect what `num_of_ports` reports. However if a single rebel brigade
# starts a 100-year siege on the capital in a country that is otherwise free of troubles, suddenly
# the whole country counts as being landlocked. (This singular behavior also includes the fact that
# occupied ports seem to be accounted for, though paths to the owner's capital are never computed
# for them.)
#
# To sidestep these quirks and spare players the frustration of spuriously invalidated CBs, a
# different requirement is used instead: `any_owned_province = { port = yes }`.

# Order that CBs are executed in a peace treaty

# Great War CB's
dismantle_cb = {
    sprite_index = 20
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

	constructing_cb = no
	always = yes
    #construction_speed = 0.25

    badboy_factor = 2
    prestige_factor = 10
    peace_cost_factor = 35
    penalty_factor = 3

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 3
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 108

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    can_use = {
		OR = {
            AND = {
                 THIS = {
			        is_greater_power = yes
		        	mass_politics = 1
		        }
		        OR = {
			        rank = 16
			        colonial_nation = yes
			        any_owned_province = { is_overseas = yes }
		        }
		        THIS = {
			        is_disarmed = no
			        NOT = {
			    	    has_country_flag = in_great_war
			    	    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
		        		has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			        }
			        NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0.99 } }
		        }
		        is_vassal = no
		        is_disarmed = no
		        OR = {
			        NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
			        war_with = THIS
		        }
		        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
		        NOT = { has_country_flag = target_of_dismantlement }
		        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
		        NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 } }
            }
            AND = {
				THIS = {
					ai = no
					has_country_flag = literally_cheating
				}
			}
        }
    }

    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_DISMANTLE_NAME

    on_add = {
        FROM = {
            set_country_flag = target_of_dismantlement
        }
		THIS = {
			country_event = 4778743
		}
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = pro_military
            to = jingoism
            value = 0.10
        }
        #country_event = 96000
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
		set_country_flag = Major_Defeated
		THIS = { set_country_flag = conference_sanity_check }
		CLN = { country_event = 4778746 }
    }
}

    }

    }
}

# Acquire Core State
acquire_core_state = {
    sprite_index = 5
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		THIS = { NOT = { has_unclaimed_cores = no } }
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        number_of_states = 1 # annex if you want their last state
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				tag = PLS
				owns = 3351
				OR = {
					THIS = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { war_with = PLS }
							tag = TUR
							ai = yes
							NOT = { year = 1850 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						ai = yes
						THIS = {
							AND = {
								NOT = { war_with = PLS }
								tag = PER
								ai = yes
								NOT = { year = 1860 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = arabistan_annexed }
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						ai = no
						THIS = {
							AND = {
								NOT = { war_with = PLS }
								tag = PER
								ai = yes
								OR = {
									NOT = { year = 1835 }
									relation = { who = PLS value = 75 }
								}
								NOT = { has_country_flag = arabistan_annexed }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = KHZ
				owns = 3351
				OR = {
					THIS = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { war_with = KHZ }
							tag = TUR
							ai = yes
							NOT = { year = 1850 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						ai = yes
						THIS = {
							AND = {
								NOT = { war_with = KHZ }
								tag = PER
								ai = yes
								NOT = { year = 1860 }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = arabistan_annexed }
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						ai = no
						THIS = {
							AND = {
								NOT = { war_with = KHZ }
								tag = PER
								ai = yes
								OR = {
									NOT = { year = 1835 }
									relation = { who = KHZ value = 75 }
								}
								NOT = { has_country_flag = arabistan_annexed }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = JOR
				owns = 934
				ai = yes
				THIS = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { war_with = JOR }
						tag = TUR
						ai = yes
						NOT = { year = 1860 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
		is_substate = no
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_CORE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        country_event = 2650    # Territorial Loss event
    }
}

restore_austrian_empire = {
    sprite_index = 21
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            tag = AUS
            OR = {
                war_policy = jingoism
                war_policy = pro_military
                war_with = THIS
            }
        }
		neighbour = AUS
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                is_core = VEN
                is_core = SLO
                is_core = SLV
                is_core = BOH
                is_core = HUN
                is_core = GLM
                region = AUS_771
                region = AUS_780
                region = AUS_777
                region = AUS_654
                region = AUS_647
                region = AUS_652
                region = AUS_657
            }
			NOT = { province_id = 742 } #Neum
			NOT = { province_id = 741 } #Neum
			NOT = { province_id = 743 } #Neum
			NOT = { province_id = 3277 } #Hultschin/Hlucin/Hlucin
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { tag = ITA }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = accepts_italy } }
        }
        THIS = {
            rank = 16
            OR = {
                government = absolute_empire
                government = semi_constitutional_empire
                government = constitutional_empire
                government = fascist_dictatorship
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = austrian_greater_germany }
        }
        NOT = {
			tag = HUN
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
			has_global_flag = outside_cores_removed
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        NOT = { in_sphere = THIS }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ai_demand_sigmaringen }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = outside_cores_removed }
		THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
		NOT = {
			tag = PLC
			tag = PLR
			tag = POL
		}
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                is_core = VEN
                is_core = SLO
                is_core = SLV
                is_core = BOH
                is_core = HUN
                is_core = GLM
                region = AUS_702
                region = AUS_771
                region = AUS_780
                region = AUS_777
                region = AUS_654
				region = AUS_647
                region = AUS_652
                region = AUS_657
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_AUSTRIAN_EMPIRE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                is_core = KRA
                is_core = GLM
            }
            remove_core = KRA
        }
    }

}

    sprite_index = 21
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.7
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

			}

					NOT = { num_of_cities = 5 }
				}

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1

# Unification Demand State
unification_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = no
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            culture_has_union_tag = yes
            is_cultural_union = no
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            AND = {
                is_culture_group = THIS
                war_with = THIS
                part_of_sphere = no
                THIS = { NOT = { tag = AUS } }
                THIS = { NOT = { tag = KUK } }
                THIS = { NOT = { tag = DNB } }
                THIS = { NOT = { tag = UBD } }
            }
            NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS }
        }
        any_state = {
            any_owned_province = {
                any_core = {
                    this_culture_union = this_union
                    is_cultural_union = yes
                }
            }
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { tag = PRU }
        NOT = { tag = NGF }
        THIS = { NOT = { tag = KUK } }
        THIS = { NOT = { tag = DNB } }
        THIS = { NOT = { tag = UBD } }
    }
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_core = {
                this_culture_union = this_union
                is_cultural_union = yes
                NOT = { tag = SIE }
            }
        }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                RHI = { exists = yes }
                RHI = { vassal_of = FRA }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_UNIFICATION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

            is_greater_power = yes

            culture_has_union_tag = yes

            THIS = {

                    year = 1860

                        has_country_modifier = prussian_general_staff
                        NOT = { war_exhaustion = 1 }
                    }
                }
                ai = yes
            }
            THIS = { NOT = { tag = PRU } }

        }
        OR = {

            }
            war_with = THIS
        }

        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }
    po_clear_union_sphere = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 2.0 # battle score twice that of oppenent

    war_name = UNIFICATION_HUMILIATE_NAME

            to = pro_military

		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        prestige_factor = -0.2
        country_event = 99996
    }
}

        NOT = {
            tag = FROM
            FROM = { tag = THIS }
            FROM = { tag = MTC }
            this_culture_union = FROM
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = ETH }
                NOT = { exists = ETH }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = BOL }
                exists = PBC
            }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                    THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
                    THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
                    has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
                    has_global_flag = persia_treaty
                    THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
                    has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
                }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
                        any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = no }
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						any_owned_province = {
							is_core = FROM
							OR = {
								any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
								any_neighbor_province = {
									owner = {
										OR = {
											in_sphere = THIS
											alliance_with = THIS
										}
									}
								}
								controlled_by = THIS
							}
						}
						FROM = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = europe
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								continent = north_america
								continent = south_america
							}
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								continent = north_america
								continent = south_america
							}
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = asia } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = asia
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = indochina } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = indochina
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = africa } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = africa
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = oceania } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = oceania
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = australia_new_zealand
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = polynesia } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = polynesia
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { is_culture_group = THIS }
						any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
					}
				}
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { exists = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                involved_in_crisis = yes
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                }
            }
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                exists = yes
                is_cultural_union = no
                involved_in_crisis = yes
            }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { civilized = yes }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
            has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
            has_global_flag = persia_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
            has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { exists = no }
            FROM = { alliance_with = THIS }
            FROM = { in_sphere = THIS }
            FROM = { relation = { who = THIS value = 100 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            AND = {
                tag = EGY
                THIS = { has_country_flag = oriental_crisis_support_OE }
                FROM = { tag = TUR }
            }
            tag = AFG
            THIS = { has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
            has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = persia_treaty }
            has_global_flag = persia_treaty
            THIS = { has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam }
            has_global_flag = intervention_in_vietnam
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #Prevent the CB being used on substates and on countries you are at war with
        NOT = {
            FROM = { war_with = THIS }
            FROM = { is_substate = yes }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
    }
    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes
    po_release_puppet = yes

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { ai = no } }
            owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = disable_conquest_cb duration = -1 } }
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = { remove_country_modifier = disable_conquest_cb }
        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = TUR owns = 846 has_global_flag = italy_fights_turk war_with = ITA } }
            ITA = { country_event = 900009 }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = TUR NOT = { owns = 846 } has_global_flag = italy_fights_turk war_with = ITA } }
            ITA = { country_event = 900109 }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = RUS has_global_flag = wakhan_treaty } }
            RUS = { clr_global_flag = wakhan_treaty }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { tag = RUS has_global_flag = persia_treaty } }
            RUS = { clr_global_flag = persia_treaty }
        }
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

        }

    }
}

monroe_doctrine = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.0

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.5
    penalty_factor = 0.5

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48
    always = yes

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            tag = USA
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                continent = south_america
                continent = north_america
            }

                OR = {
					AND = {
						is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
						NOT = { primary_culture = caribeno }
					}
                    AND = {
                        tag = CUB
						USA = { has_country_flag = maine_incident }
                    }
                    primary_culture = mayan
                }

            NOT = {
                is_core = USA
                region = ENG_1979 #Guayana

                province_id = 2200
				province_id = 3393
				province_id = 2236
				province_id = 3340 #Fort Ross
            }
        }
        THIS = {
            government = democracy
            is_greater_power = yes
        }

            capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
            capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
        }

            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }

        }

            OR = {
                exists = yes
                is_cultural_union = no
            }
            OR = {
				AND = {
					is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
					NOT = { primary_culture = caribeno }
				}
                primary_culture = mayan
                AND = {
                    tag = CUB
					USA = { has_country_flag = maine_incident }
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = { tag = FROM }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM

			NOT = {

		is_vassal = yes
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }

            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
				has_country_modifier = neutrality
            }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope

	po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military

# Cut Down to size
cut_down_to_size = {
    sprite_index = 8

    badboy_factor = 1.3
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 25
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = CUT_DOWN_TO_SIZE_WAR_NAME

    can_use = {
        THIS = { civilized = yes }
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = { OR = { vassal_of = THIS substate_of = THIS in_sphere = THIS } }
        }
        is_disarmed = no
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
		NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    civilized = no
                    OR = {
                        owns = 1498 #Macao
                        owns = 1538 #Shanghai
						owns = 3364 #Sanmen
						owns = 1961 #Chusan
                        owns = 1496 #Hong Kong
                        owns = 1566    #Qingdao
                        owns = 1481 #Lushun - Port Arthur
                        owns = 1569 #Weihaiwei
                        owns = 1606 #Jiaxing
                        owns = 2681 #Taibei
                        owns = 2562 #Tainan
                        owns = 1499 #Hainan
                        owns = 2632 #Kwangchowan
                        #owns = 1540 #Nantong
                        owns = 1071 #Qeshm
                        owns = 1695 #Ifni
						owns = 3682 #Tarfaya
						owns = 3841 #Juzur Khuriya Muriya
						owns = 3967 #Barbara
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                    NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            owner = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two }
							has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two
							duration = 30
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty
								has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = negotiating_unequal_treaty
							duration = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			THIS = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_country_modifier = negotiating_treaty
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = negotiating_treaty_two duration = 30 }
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = negotiating_treaty }
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = negotiating_treaty duration = 30 }
					}
				}
			}
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no has_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism } }
            owner = { remove_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no NOT = { has_country_modifier = western_influences } } }
            owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = western_influences duration = -1 } }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no NOT = { capital_scope = { has_country_modifier = legation_quarter } } } }
            owner = { capital_scope = { add_province_modifier = { name = legation_quarter duration = -1 } } }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = holding_tangiers owns = 1686 } }
            owner = { 1686 = { secede_province = THIS } clr_country_flag = holding_tangiers }
            THIS = { 1686 = { secede_province = MOR } }
        }
        random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = refused_to_cede_congo } }
            owner = { any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CNG } secede_province = THIS } clr_country_flag = refused_to_cede_congo }
            THIS = { any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CNG } secede_province = CNG } }
        }

        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = { has_country_flag = lied_about_congo }
                THIS = { has_country_flag = claiming_congo }
            }
            owner = {
                any_country = { clr_country_flag = claiming_congo }
                clr_country_flag = lied_about_congo
                any_owned = {
                    limit = { is_core = CNG }
                    secede_province = THIS
                }
            }
        }
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }

    }

great_game_cb = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.35
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes
    po_make_puppet = yes
    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 1.0

    war_name = WAR_PUPPET_NAME

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            OR = {
                tag = ENG
                tag = RUS
            }
        }
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS }
        }
        civilized = no
        is_vassal = no
        war = no
        OR = {
            AND = {
				OR = {
					tag = KOK
					tag = KHI
					tag = BUK 
					tag = BDK
					tag = KYR
				}
				THIS = { tag = RUS }
			}
            AND = { tag = PNJ has_global_flag = 1_anglo_sikh_war }
            AND = { tag = BHU has_country_flag = anglo_bhutan_war }
            AND = {
                tag = AFG
                THIS = { tag = RUS NOT = { has_global_flag = afghanistan_is_neutral } }
                KOK = {
                    all_core = {
                        OR = {
                            owned_by = THIS
                            owner = {
                                vassal_of = THIS
                                war = no
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                BUK = {
                    all_core = {
                        OR = {
                            owned_by = THIS
                            owner = {
                                vassal_of = THIS
                                war = no
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                1208 = { OR = { owned_by = THIS owner = { vassal_of = THIS war = no } } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
		THIS = {
            has_country_flag = monarchy_government
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = no_more_great_game
                has_country_modifier = punitive_effects
                badboy = 0.85
            }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
		}
        NOT = {
            has_global_flag = british_dismantled
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            truce_with = THIS
            in_sphere = THIS
        }
    }

    on_add = {
        badboy = 3.5

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = MAK
						tag = KAL
						tag = LAS
					}
				}
			}
			THIS = { badboy = -2.5 }
		}

        random_country = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    tag = RUS
                    tag = ENG
                }
                NOT = { tag = THIS }
            }
            relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 19370
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Humiliate
humiliate = {
    sprite_index = 11
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 15
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		OR = {
			prestige = 10
			THIS = { ai = no }
		}
		OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
			THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
			THIS = { ai = no }
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
			THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
			THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
			war_with = THIS
			THIS = { ai = no }
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
			THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
			THIS = { ai = no }
		}
		THIS = {
            total_amount_of_divisions = 1
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
		OR = {
			THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
			war_with = THIS
		}
		#AI GP's will not invoke Humiliate when they have Unification Humiliate available
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				culture_has_union_tag = yes
				is_culture_group = THIS
				is_greater_power = yes
				cultural_union = { exists = no }
				NOT = { has_cultural_sphere = yes }
				THIS = {
					ai = yes
					is_greater_power = yes
					nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
				}
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                is_greater_power = no
            }
        }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 2.0

    war_name = WAR_HUMILIATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		prestige_factor = -0.28
		prestige = -25
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

#Acquire colonial state CB's
place_in_the_sun = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1.1
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = yes }
        THIS = {
            OR = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        NOT = { owned_by = THIS }
                        is_colonial = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        #AI Pacifist will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = pacifism } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI Anti Military will not use this commonly
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } }
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI after the Berlin Conference will need to hate each other guts to use this
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_global_flag = berlin_conference }
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = yes }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                any_core = { civilized = no }
            }
            any_owned_province = { continent = africa }
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    OR = {
                        any_core = { exists = yes }
                        any_core = { exists = no }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}
            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }
            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        rank = 16
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }
            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
        }
        # #AI countries will avoid taking new world colonies (e.g. from Argentina) when not proper
        # OR = {
            # THIS = { ai = no }
            # THIS = {
                # capital_scope = {
                    # NOT = {
                        # continent = europe
                        # continent = asia
                        # continent = africa
                    # }
                # }
            # }
            # any_owned_province = {
                # NOT = {
                    # continent = north_america
                    # continent = south_america
                # }
            # }
            # any_owned_province = { NOT = { any_core = { has_country_flag = new_world_nation } } }
            # any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            # any_owned_province = { terrain = new_world_small_island }
            # any_owned_province = { terrain = new_world_arctic }
            # any_owned_province = {
                # OR = {
                    # is_core = CUB
                    # is_core = HAI
                    # is_core = DOM
                    # is_core = CAN
                # }
            # }

        # }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                port = yes
                any_neighbor_province = { owner = { tag = THIS } }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_COLONIAL_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Gain control of State
acquire_state = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            civilized = yes
            THIS = { civilized = no }
        }
        any_state = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            war_with = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
		is_substate = no
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
		OR = {
			NOT = { year = 1860 }
			THIS = { civilized = no }
		}
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI anti military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI will not use this CB when duking it out over hegemony
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    is_greater_power = yes
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }
        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }
            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        rank = 16
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }
            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
        }
        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group and they're pro-military
        #jingoistic countries will also take states with existing cores that they also own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        #Countries can't take capitals or cores (except cores in SW before 1834)
        NOT = {
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
                NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = sw_set
						NOT = { year = 1834 }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
					}
				}
			}
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

acquire_state_mid = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		year = 1860
		NOT = { year = 1880 }
		THIS = { civilized = yes }
		civilized = yes
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            war_with = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        any_state = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI anti military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI will not use this CB when duking it out over hegemony
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    is_greater_power = yes
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
		THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        rank = 16
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group and they're pro-military
        #jingoistic countries will also take states with existing cores that they also own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        #Countries can't take capitals or cores
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Gain control of State
acquire_state_late = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.1
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.45
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		year = 1880
		THIS = { civilized = yes }
		civilized = yes
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            war_with = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        any_state = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI anti military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #AI will not use this CB when duking it out over hegemony
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    culture_has_union_tag = yes
                    is_culture_group = THIS
                    cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    is_greater_power = yes
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {

        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        rank = 16
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group and they're pro-military
        #jingoistic countries will also take states with existing cores that they also own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        #Countries can't take capitals or cores
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Chinese Reunification
china_acquire_state = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 84

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_culture_group = east_asian
        }
		neighbour = THIS
        OR = {
            is_culture_group = east_asian
            any_owned_province = {
                is_core = CHI
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_global_flag = warlord_era_has_begun }
            NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
            owns = 1616
            AND = {
                tag = CHI
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = neutral_faction } }
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction } }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = TPG
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = neutral_faction } }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KMT
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = neutral_faction } }
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction } }
                THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = communist_faction } }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { tag = TPG }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = beiyang_faction
                    has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction
                    has_country_flag = communist_faction
                    tag = KMT
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction has_country_flag = communist_faction tag = CHI tag = KMT } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { tag = KMT }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = beiyang_faction
                    tag = CHI
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction tag = CHI tag = TPG } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = beiyang_faction
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = beiyang_faction tag = CHI tag = TPG } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = kuomintang_faction tag = TPG tag = KMT } } } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { has_country_flag = communist_faction }
                OR = {
                    has_country_flag = communist_faction
                    THIS = { NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = communist_faction tag = TPG tag = CHI } } } }
                }
            }
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                war_policy = pacifism
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                year = 1900
                any_owned_province = {
                    NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                    is_core = CHI
                    owner = { civilized = yes }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                    is_core = CHI
                }
            }
            any_owned_province = {
                is_core = CHI
                owner = { civilized = no }
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            }
            any_owned_province = {
                owner = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                NOT = { is_core = CHI }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CHINA_REUNIFICATION

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.10
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

sahel_jihad_cb = {
    sprite_index = 29
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.25

    badboy_factor = 2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            primary_culture = fulbe
            civilized = no
        }
        civilized = no
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        THIS = { 
            OR = {
				has_country_flag = monarchy_government
                government = theocracy
            }
		}
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_flag = sunni_country }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = { owner = { war_with = THIS } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_SAHEL_JIHAD_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
