# Demand Concession
demand_concession_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    construction_speed = 1.2
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        civilized = no
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = { port = yes }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
				OR = {
					THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
					THIS = { ai = no }
				}
			}
            AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = QNG }
				NOT = { tag = KOR }
				NOT = { tag = MCK }
			}
			THIS = { primary_culture = japanese }
			THIS = { primary_culture = russian }
			THIS = { ai = no }
		}
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                civilization_progress = 0.6
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            war_with = THIS
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { primary_culture = japanese }
            }
            THIS = { civilized = yes ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        THIS = { 
            NOT = { nationalism_n_imperialism = 1 }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = berlin_conference }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
			#Player can take any state neighboring their vassal
			AND = {
				THIS = { ai = no }
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								substate_of = THIS
								vassal_of = THIS
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa
            continent = east_africa
            continent = south_africa
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
			owner = { has_country_flag = indian_tag }
            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
            }

            AND = {
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }

    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Bad Boy
rude_boy = {
    sprite_index = 28
    is_triggered_only = no
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 2
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 1.5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        badboy = 1
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				government = radical_republic
				THIS = { government = radical_republic }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
        is_disarmed = no
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier } }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes
    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_RUDEBOI_NAME

    on_add = {
		prestige_factor = -0.28
		prestige = -25
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					badboy = 1 #25 due to condition being different from effect
				}
			}
			owner = {
				badboy = -1000
				badboy = 24.99
			}
		}
	}
}

# Conquest
conquest = {
    sprite_index = 2
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = { port = yes }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
				OR = {
					THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
					THIS = { ai = no }
				}
			}
            AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                any_state = {
                    is_colonial = no
                    NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        government = proletarian_dictatorship
                        government = fascist_dictatorship
                    }

                }
                NOT = { number_of_states = 4 }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = SWI
                NOT = { number_of_states = 4 }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI anti-military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI will not use this when fighting for hegemony
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                    any_greater_power = {
                        war_with = THIS
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        is_culture_group = THIS
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    }
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    rank = 16
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group
        #jingoistic will also grab existing cores that they already own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { total_pops = 400000 }
				NOT = { number_of_states = 3 }
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                has_country_modifier = disable_conquest_cb
            }
        }
    }

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 5
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONQUEST_NAME
}

# Berlin Conference
annex_africa = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.5

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 2

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            has_global_flag = berlin_conference
			colonial_nation = yes
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            slavery = no_slavery
            civilized = yes
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        civilized = no
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        #Claimed colonial regions can't be conquered with this CB
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = colonial_railroading_disabled
			NOT = { THIS = { tag = POR ai = yes } }
		}
        NOT = { has_country_flag = cfs_owner }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        THIS = { 
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality }
            NOT = { tag = RUS }
            NOT = { tag = TUR }
		}
        NOT = {
            tag = MOR
            tag = ALD
            tag = TRI
            tag = CYR
            tag = LIB
            tag = ETH
            tag = MAD
            tag = EGY
            has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
        }
        ai = yes
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

			colonial_nation = yes

        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {

            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }

        #Claimed colonial regions can't be conquered with this CB
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = colonial_railroading_disabled
			NOT = { THIS = { tag = POR ai = yes } }
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { number_of_states = 2 }
        THIS = { 
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = claimed_africa }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = cfs_master }
            NOT = { tag = RUS }
            NOT = { tag = TUR }
		}
        NOT = {
            tag = MOR
            tag = ALD
            tag = TRI
            tag = LIB
            tag = CYR
            primary_culture = kefficho
            primary_culture = amhara
            primary_culture = tigray
            primary_culture = oromo
            primary_culture = harari
            has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
        }
        ai = yes
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_PROTECTORATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 120 }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = { add_country_modifier = { name = claimed_africa duration = 120 } }
        tech_school = unciv_tech_school
    }
}

# Establish Protectorate
establish_protectorate_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
		THIS = {
            civilized = yes
        }
		civilized = no
		OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            war_with = THIS
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { tag = JAP }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
			owner = { has_country_flag = indian_tag }
            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
            }

            AND = {
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

        THIS = {
			NOT = {
				nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
				has_global_flag = berlin_conference
				has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			}
		}
        NOT = {
			is_our_vassal = THIS
			has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			number_of_states = 2
		}
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_PROTECTORATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
    on_po_accepted = { tech_school = unciv_tech_school }
}

negotiated_transfer = {
    sprite_index = 5
    is_triggered_only = yes

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 0
    penalty_factor = 0

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    construction_speed = 1000.0

    can_use = {
        THIS = { ai = no }
        ai = no
        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        is_vassal = no
    }

    allowed_states = {
        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_NEGOTIATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.00
        }
    }
}

egyptian_ottoman_war = {
    sprite_index = 35
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 40
    penalty_factor = 0
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 0
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

	po_status_quo = yes

    war_name = WAR_EGYPT_OTTOMAN_NAME

    can_use = {
    }

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		THIS = {
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
					}
				}
				owner = {
					country_event = 184822731
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp }
					}
				}

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = SYKES_PICOT_WAR_NAME

    on_add = {

            from = jingoism

		prestige_factor = -0.28

    }
}

# Make Puppet
make_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 2.0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		total_pops = 400000
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = {
                OR = {
                    vassal_of = THIS
                    substate_of = THIS
                    in_sphere = THIS
                }
            }
        }
        is_vassal = no
        is_greater_power = no
        OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { total_pops = 5000000 }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
		THIS = {
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
		}
		NOT = {
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            is_our_vassal = THIS
		}
		ai = yes
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope

    po_make_puppet = yes

    war_name = WAR_PUPPET_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 19370
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Make Puppet

    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		total_pops = 100000
		NOT = {
			total_pops = 400000
		}
        is_vassal = no
        is_greater_power = no
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }

        }

            }

            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }

            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
		ai = yes
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope

# Become Independent
become_independent = {
    sprite_index = 10
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    always = yes

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 108

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            THIS = { substate_of = FROM }
        }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        NOT = { AND = { tag = EGY ai = yes } }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        OR = {
            FROM = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
            war_with = THIS
        }
    }

    po_release_puppet = yes
    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    war_name = WAR_INDEPENDENCE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
        add_war_goal = {
            casus_belli = make_puppet
        }
        leave_alliance = FROM
        release_vassal = THIS
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Revert from Communist Government
uninstall_communist_gov_cb = {
    sprite_index = 13
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    # Is automatically added to countries that intervened at while install_communist_gov_cb
    # so they can revert those countries government.
    constructing_cb = no

    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        government = proletarian_dictatorship
        OR = {
            THIS = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                }
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        THIS = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
    }

    po_uninstall_communist_gov_type = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

great_war_install_democracy = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1.5
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 30
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1
    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            has_country_flag = in_great_war
            OR = {
                government = hms_government
                government = constitutional_empire
                government = democracy
            }
        }
        civilized = yes
        has_country_flag = in_great_war
        war_with = THIS
        OR = {
            government = proletarian_dictatorship
            government = fascist_dictatorship
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		prestige_factor = -0.28
		prestige = -25
        THIS = { set_country_flag = friendly_democracy }
        country_event = 96085
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

install_democracy = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1.5
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 50
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        has_global_flag = great_wars_enabled
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
        }
        civilized = yes
        OR = {
            government = proletarian_dictatorship
            government = fascist_dictatorship
        }
        THIS = { 
            OR = {
                government = hms_government
                government = constitutional_empire
                government = democracy
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war }
		}
        OR = {
            THIS = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = in_great_war
                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                }
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = DEMOCRACY_WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		prestige_factor = -0.28
		prestige = -25
        THIS = {
            set_country_flag = friendly_democracy
            any_country = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        government = proletarian_dictatorship
                        government = fascist_dictatorship
                    }
                }
                relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
            }
        }
        country_event = 96085
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

        civilized = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = in_great_war
                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes
    po_install_communist_gov_type = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		prestige_factor = -0.28
		prestige = -25
        THIS = {
            set_country_flag = friendly_communist
            any_country = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        government = hms_government
                        government = constitutional_empire
                        government = democracy
                    }
                }
                relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
            }
        }
        country_event = 96087
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Gain control of Substate region
acquire_substate_region = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = { ai = no }
        num_of_substates = 1 # if has any substate
        any_substate = {
            OR = {
				neighbour = THIS
                AND = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            number_of_states = 1
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                is_colonial = no
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_substate_regions = {
        is_colonial = no
        #owner = { NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } }
        any_owned_province = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_SUBSTATE_REGION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Dismantle fortifications (forts + naval bases)
dismantle_forts = {
    sprite_index = 16

    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1

    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    # THIS - us

                THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    po_destroy_forts = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

#Placeholder for acquire state-by-event
acquire_any_state = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 0
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

	always = no

    can_use = {
        is_vassal = no
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #Countries can't take capitals
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }
        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }
        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
			#Player in MP can take anything they want from other players
			AND = {
				owner = { ai = no }
				THIS = { ai = no }
				has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
			}

            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        rank = 16
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    civilized = no
                    is_culture_group = east_asian
                    OR = {
                        owns = 1481
                        owns = 1496
                        owns = 1498
                        owns = 1538
						owns = 3364
						owns = 1961
                        owns = 1566
                        owns = 1569
                        owns = 1606
                        owns = 2632
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                    NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            owner = { country_event = 1316089 }
        }
    }
}

                    }
                }
            }
			owner = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two }
							has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty
								has_country_modifier = negotiating_unequal_treaty_two
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = negotiating_unequal_treaty
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
            THIS = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_country_modifier = negotiating_treaty
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = negotiating_treaty_two duration = -1 }
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = negotiating_treaty }
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = negotiating_treaty duration = -1 }
					}
				}
			}
        }
        #random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no has_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism } }
        #    owner = { remove_country_modifier = uncivilized_isolationism }
        #}
        #random_owned = { limit = { owner = { civilized = no NOT = { has_country_modifier = western_influences } } }
        #    owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = western_influences duration = -1 } }

        #}
    }

end_radicals = {
    sprite_index = 37
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 5
    prestige_factor = 4
    peace_cost_factor = 75
    penalty_factor = 1
	always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		government = radical_republic
        civilized = yes
		is_vassal = no
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            war_with = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			AND = {
				tag = PRG
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
		THIS = {
			NOT = {
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				government = democracy
				government = radical_republic
				ruling_party_ideology = radical
			}
		}
    }

	po_add_to_sphere = yes
	po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_END_RADICALS_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		prestige_factor = -0.28
		prestige = -25
		set_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
		THIS = {
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = conservative
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = conservative
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = socialist
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = socialist
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = communist
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = communist
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {

					}
				}
				owner = {

					}

			random_owned = {

						}
						government = absolute_monarchy
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {

						OR = {
							government = semi_constitutional_empire

					}

#Colonial Conquest/Imperialism CB
colonial_conquest = {
    sprite_index = 21
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.25
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            state_n_government = 1
            civilized = yes
            OR = {
                AND = {
					capital_scope = { continent = europe }
                    NOT = {
                        tag = TUR
                        tag = RUS
                    }
                }
                tech_school = naval_tech_school
                tech_school = japanese_tech_school
            }
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        civilized = no
        exists = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
			neighbour = THIS
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 150 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { badboy = 0.88 } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
		THIS = {
            is_disarmed = no
            NOT = { war_policy = pacifism }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = claimed_africa }
		}
        OR = {
            #Mozambique
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    capital_scope = { continent = europe }
                    OR = {
                        NOT = { has_global_flag = berlin_conference }
                        NOT = { nationalism_n_imperialism = 1 }
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_country_flag = reconquest_of_lourenco_marques
                        AND = {
                            owns = 2060
                            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
                        }
                    }
                }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        region = POR_2060

    badboy_factor = 0.2
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        war_with = THIS
		THIS = {
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
		}
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            has_country_modifier = no_more_war
            has_country_flag = in_great_war
        }
    }

    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME_REPARATIONS

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    tag = HAI
                    FRA = { is_greater_power = yes }
                    NOT = { has_country_flag = agreed_to_pay_debt }
                }
            }
            owner = {
                country_event = 45108
            }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    tag = MEX
                    has_country_flag = pay_1st_pastry_war
                }
            }
            owner = {
                country_event = 45108
            }
        }
    }
}

USS_monroe = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no
    constructing_cb = no

    always = yes


    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.5
    penalty_factor = 0.5

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            is_greater_power = yes
            has_country_flag = formed_USS
            has_country_flag = USS_miranda
        }
        OR = {
            is_culture_group = american_cultures
            is_culture_group = neo_european_cultures
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = asia }
            capital_scope = { continent = oceania }
            capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
            capital_scope = { continent = polynesia }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                continent = south_america
                continent = north_america
            }
            any_core = {
                OR = {
                    is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
                    primary_culture = afro_latino
                    primary_culture = afro_brazilian
                }
            }
            NOT = {
                is_core = THIS
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        NOT = { tag = FROM }
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
            NOT = { has_global_flag = the_call_for_south_american_union }
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
                primary_culture = afro_latino
                primary_culture = afro_brazilian
            }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
            OR = {
                continent = north_america
                continent = south_america
            }
        }
    }
    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes
    po_release_puppet = yes

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
}

#Take Capital
take_capital = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 3
    prestige_factor = 10
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 36

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        any_owned_province = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
        }
        is_vassal = no
        OR = {
			neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                civilized = yes
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                }
            }
            AND = {
                civilized = no
                THIS = {
                    civilized = no
                }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = in_great_war
                has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1834 }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = battle_royale_set }
            }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        is_colonial = no
        any_owned_province = {
            is_colonial = no
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
        }
        any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

			}

        }
        OR = {

		}

					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering

            continent = south_africa

                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }

                        ai = yes

                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }

                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
            }

                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }

                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }

                    army_risk_management = 1
                }

                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {

                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }

                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }

			neighbour = THIS
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = { port = yes }
				THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
				OR = {
					THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
					THIS = { ai = no }
				}
			}
            AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = in_great_war
                has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
				has_global_flag = berlin_conference
				nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }
        any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { tag = THIS }
				}
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa
            continent = east_africa
            continent = south_africa
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
			owner = { has_country_flag = indian_tag }
            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
            }

            AND = {
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

    }


    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Liberate puppet
liberate_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.3

    badboy_factor = 2.8
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1


    can_use = {
        THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality
			has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality } }
		ai = yes
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        FROM = { exists = no }
        OR = {
            is_releasable_vassal = FROM
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { NOT = { any_core = { is_core = THIS } } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
						any_owned_province = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								owner = { tag = THIS }
							}
						}
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
						any_owned_province = {
							is_core = FROM
							any_neighbor_province = {
								owner = {
									OR = {
										in_sphere = THIS
										alliance_with = THIS
										tag = THIS
									}
								}
							}
							controlled_by = THIS
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = europe
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								continent = north_america
								continent = south_america
							}
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								continent = north_america
								continent = south_america
							}
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = asia } }
						any_owned_province = {
							continent = asia
							is_core = FROM
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { is_culture_group = THIS }
						any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                is_cultural_union = no
                involved_in_crisis = yes
            }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            FROM = { civilized = yes }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
        }
        NOT = {
            tag = FROM
            FROM = { tag = THIS }
            FROM = { tag = MTC }
            this_culture_union = FROM
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = ETH }
                NOT = { exists = ETH }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = BOL }
                exists = PBC
            }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
        }
    }
    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                exists = no
                has_country_flag = existing_country
            }
            clr_country_flag = existing_country
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                exists = no
                has_country_flag = vassal_nation_cb
            }
            clr_country_flag = vassal_nation_cb
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event
        THIS = { country_event = 19369 } # Starts puppeting event chain
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

abolish_sound_dues_cb = {

    peace_cost_factor = 25
    penalty_factor = 1

    crisis = no

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = ABOLISH_SOUND_DUES_CB_WAR_NAME

    can_use = {
    }

    on_add = {

            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
